  api: {

    rgx: function rgx(str) {

      var regex = new RegExp(str);

      return regex;

    }

  },

  elements: {

    checkForElement: function checkForElement(element, callback) {

      var el = element;

      var interval = setInterval(function (e) {

        var theElement = document.getElementById(el) || document.querySelectorAll(el);

        if (theElement.length === 0 || theElement === null) return;

        callback();

        clearInterval(interval);

      }, 400);

    },

    transformToArray: function transformToArray(el) {

      el = [].slice.apply(el);

      return el;

    },

    onBody: function onBody(bool, str) {

      if (bool) {

        document.body.classList.add(str);

      } else {

        document.body.classList.remove(str);

      }

    },

    createContainer: function createContainer(htmltag, strclass) {

      var innerInfo = arguments.length > 2 && arguments[2] !== undefined ? arguments[2] : '';

      var a = document.createElement(htmltag);

      a.className = strclass;

      a.innerHTML = innerInfo;

      return a;

    }

  },

  url: {

    checkUrlParams: function checkUrlParams(url, param) {

      var urlAccepted;

      var params = param;



      if (url.includes(params)) {

        urlAccepted = true;

      }



      return urlAccepted;

    }

  },

  network: {

    intercepter: function intercepter(callback) {

      var oldXHROpen = window.XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open;



      window.XMLHttpRequest.prototype.open = function (method, url, async, user, password) {

        // do something with the method, url and etc.

        this.addEventListener('load', function (e) {

          //console.log('load: ' + this.responseURL);

          var thisResponse = this.response === '' || this.reponse === undefined ? this.response : JSON.parse(this.response);

          callback(this.readyState, this.responseURL, thisResponse);

        });

        return oldXHROpen.apply(this, arguments);

      };

    },

    validateIntercep: function validateIntercep(state, element, url) {

      var pageValid = false;



      try {

        if (state !== 4) return;

        var checkHttpRequest = tools.api.rgx('confirm-your-order').test(url);

        if (!checkHttpRequest) return;

        var deliverySummary = document.getElementById(element);

        if (!deliverySummary.length) return;

        pageValid = true;

      } catch (e) {

        console.log('problem in validatePage(fn)/delivery -', e);

      }



      return pageValid;

    }

  },

  validate: {

    checkForMobile: function checkForMobile() {

      var windoWidth = window.innerWidth;

      var itsOkay;

      if (windoWidth < 521) itsOkay = true;

      return itsOkay;

    }

  },

  str: {

    removeSpecial: function removeSpecial(str) {

      return str.normalize('NFD').replace(/[^\w\s]/gi, '');

    }

  }

};

    seekAndDestroy: function(){

        var seekConstantly = setInterval(function(){

            var firstLevelMenu = document.querySelector('.firstLevelMenu__desktop');

            if(firstLevelMenu){

                var a = firstLevelMenu.querySelectorAll('li[class*="jsx-"]');

                var applySliceElement = [].slice.apply(a);

        }, 400);

    }

var ui = {

    findNodesToInsert: function() {

        var secondLevelItems = document.querySelectorAll('.secondLevelMenu');

        if(!secondLevelItems.length) return;

        var arrSecondlevelItems = [].slice.apply(secondLevelItems);

        // find each case

        arrSecondlevelItems.map(function(el){

            var arrSecontParent = el;

            //if(el.querySelector('.sale_ticket')) return;

            var thirdMenu = el.querySelectorAll('a[class*="thirdLevelMenu"]');

            var arrThirdMenu = [].slice.apply(thirdMenu);

            var firstArrX = arrThirdMenu[0];

            var lastArrX = arrThirdMenu[arrThirdMenu.length -2]

            if(arrThirdMenu.length){

                arrThirdMenu.map(function(el){

                    var text = el.textContent.normalize('NFD').replace(/[^\w\s]/gi, '').toLowerCase();

                    if (/nuevo/.test(text) && firstArrX.textContent === el.textContent) {

                        if(text.length >= 22) return;

                        ui.addSaleSpan(el, arrSecontParent,'sale_ticket new','NUEVO', true);

                        // thirdMenu.setAttribute('href', 'https://www.falabella.com/falabella-cl/page/Navidad-Decoracion?staticPageId=39400001');

                    }

                    if (/sale/.test(text) && lastArrX.textContent === el.textContent) {

                        if(text.length >= 22) return;

                        ui.addSaleSpan(el, arrSecontParent,'sale_ticket sale','SALE', false);

                        // thirdMenu.setAttribute('href', 'https://www.falabella.com/falabella-cl/page/Navidad-Decoracion?staticPageId=39400001');

                    } 

                });

            }

        });

    },

    addSaleSpan: function(el,parent, thisClass, thisTxt, bool){

        //var newSpan = document.createElement('span');

        //newSpan.className = 'sale_ticket new';

        //newSpan.innerText = 'NUEVO';

        //el.innerText = el.innerText.replace(/SALE/g,'').trim();

        if(bool){

            if(parent.parentElement.querySelector('.sale_ticket.new'))return;

            el.innerText = el.innerText.replace('NUEVO','').trim();

            if(el.querySelector('.sale_ticket.new'))return;

            el.appendChild(template.label(thisClass, thisTxt));

        }

        if(!bool){

            if(parent.parentElement.querySelector('.sale_ticket.sale'))return;

            var a = el.innerText.toLowerCase().replace('sale','').trim();

            el.innerText = a.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + a.slice(1);

            // el.innerText = el.innerText.replace('SALE','').trim();

            if(el.querySelector('.sale_ticket.sale'))return;

            el.appendChild(template.label(thisClass, thisTxt));

        }

    }

};

(function(){

    if(!document.querySelector('.firstLevelMenu__desktop')) return;

    window.addEventListener('click', function(e){

        if(/(arrowToggle|downArrowToggle|upArrowToggle|hamburgerBtn|icon-container-active|title|icon|line)/.test(e.target.className)){

            tool.seekAndDestroy();

        }

    });    

})();

});</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript4"](function(event, target, Promise) {

var searchSelector = 'input[class*="SearchBar"]';

var resultAreaSelector = 'div[class*="SearchList-module_searchResults"]';

var sessionStorageName = 'typeaheadresult';



function handleEvent(el) {



    var sectionText;

    var section = el.closest('section');



    var greenResult;

    var pickedElementText = el.innerText;



    var searchTerm = document.querySelector(searchSelector);





    try {

        sectionText = section.querySelector('h6').innerText

    } catch (e) {

        sectionText = 'keyword';

        greenResult = 'en negro';

    }



    var options = section.querySelector('ul').childNodes;



    var index = getIndex(el, options);



    /**

     * When index is Not a Number, the result is inside green section

     */

    if (isNaN(index)) {

        options.forEach(function(e) {

            var ul = e.querySelector('ul');

            if (ul) {

                pickedElementText = ul.parentNode.querySelector('a').innerText;

                options = ul.childNodes;

                index = getIndex(el, options);

                greenResult = 'en verde';

            }

        });

    }

    sessionStorage.setItem(sessionStorageName,

        searchTerm.value + '|' + sectionText + '|' + pickedElementText + '|' + index + '/' + options.length + (greenResult ? '|' + greenResult : '')

    );

}



function getIndex(element, list) {

    var index;

    list.forEach(function(e, i) {

        if (e.querySelector('a').href == element.href) {

            index = i;

        }

    });

    return index + 1;

}





function execute() {

    try {

        var current = 0,

            tries = 10;

        var resultArea;



        var interval = setInterval(function() {



            resultArea = document.querySelector(resultAreaSelector);



            if (resultArea) {

                var links = resultArea.querySelectorAll('a');



                links.forEach(function(l) {

                    l.addEventListener('click', function() {

                        handleEvent(l);

                    });

                });

                clearInterval(interval);

            }





            if (tries < current) {

                clearInterval(interval);

            }



            current++;

        }, 500);

    } catch (ex) {}

}





document.addEventListener('click', function() {

    execute();

});



var inputBar = document.querySelector('#testId-SearchBar-Input');

if (inputBar) {

    inputBar.addEventListener('change', function() {

        execute();

    });

}

});</script>

  <script>_satellite["_runScript10"](function(event, target, Promise) {

function fixArr(arr) {

    if (typeof (arr) === "object" && arr[0] && arr[0].skuId) {

        return arr;

    }



    if (typeof (arr) === undefined) {

        return null;

    }

    var temporalArr = [];

    if (Array.isArray(arr)) {

        temporalArr = arr;

    }

    if (typeof (arr) === "string") {

        temporalArr = arr.split(",");

    }



    var fixedArray = []

    temporalArr.forEach(function(el) {

        fixedArray.push({

            "skuId": el

        });

    });

    return fixedArray;



}



function fetchProductUpdatedInfo(skuString, callback) {



    //XMLHttpRequest

    var skuObj = fixArr(skuString);

    if (skuObj) {

        var fetchItemDetailRequest = new XMLHttpRequest();

        var fetchItemDetailURL = "/s/browse/v1/fetchItemDetails/co?" + encodeURIComponent(JSON.stringify({

            "products": skuObj

        }));



        fetchItemDetailRequest.addEventListener('load', function(event) {



                var response = JSON.parse(this.responseText);

                if (response.success && response.success === true) {

                    var filteredProducts = response.products.map(function(el) {

                        if (el.product.published !== false && el.product.purchasable !== false) {



                            var tempEl = {};

                            tempEl.id = el.product.id;

                            tempEl.prices = el.product.prices;

                            tempEl.prices.forEach(function(el2) {

                                el2.price = el2.originalPrice||el2.formattedLowestPrice;

                                delete el2.originalPrice;

                                delete el2.label;

                                delete el2.isLoyalty;

                                delete el2.opportunidadUnica;

                                delete el2.symbol;



                            });

                            return tempEl;



                        }

                    });

                  if(callback){

                       callback(filteredProducts);

                  }else{

                    console.log(filteredProducts);

                  }





                }



                if (response.success && response.success === false && callback) {

                     callback(null);



                }

        });



        fetchItemDetailRequest.open("GET", fetchItemDetailURL, true);

        fetchItemDetailRequest.send();

    }

}



window.fetchProductUpdatedInfo=fetchProductUpdatedInfo;

});</script>

function getProd() {



	var prodsArr = []

	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {

		var tempObj = {

			'sku': el.sku,

			'price': el.price,

			'quantity': el.quantity

		};

		prodsArr.push(tempObj);

	});

	return prodsArr;

}



function getTotal() {

	var total = 0;

	digitalData.ecom.productList.forEach(function (el) {

		total = el.price + total;

	})

	return total;

}

  <script>_satellite["_runScript13"](function(event, target, Promise) {

function checkForDigitalData(callback){

    var interval = setInterval(function(e){

        var theElement = window.digitalData;

        if(theElement.length === 0 || theElement === null) return;

        callback();

        clearInterval(interval);

    }, 400);

}



function modifyDigitalData(data) {

    checkForDigitalData(function(){

        var digitalData = window.digitalData;

        digitalData.login = data.login;

        digitalData.page.loginStatus = data.page.loginStatus;

    });

}



function checkIfStoredAnalytics() {

    var localStorageAnalytics = localStorage.getItem('analyticsInfo');

    if (localStorageAnalytics) {

        modifyDigitalData(JSON.parse(localStorageAnalytics));

    }

}



if (_satellite.getVar('storageCheck')) {

    checkIfStoredAnalytics();

}

});</script>

}

/**

 * @returns {Boolean} true if out of domain

function isOutOfDomain(element) {

    if (element && element.tagName === 'A') {

        var url = element.href;

        url = url.indexOf('?') != -1 ? url.substring(0, url.indexOf('?')) : url;

        if (/falabella.com/.test(url)) {

            return false;

        } else if (/mi-cuenta\/giftcards/.test(url)) {

            return true;

        }

        return true;

    }

    return false;

}

    secondLevelDescription: function(theParent) {

    order: function order(el, type) {

            thirdLevelContainer, thirdLevelLinkArr, clickedThirdLevel;

        var columnOrder = function() {

                if (ui.isSLP()) {

                    return el.innerText.split("\n", 1)[0];

                if (windowW) {

                    return linkTo;

                            switch (type) {

                                    order = indexColumn;

                                default:

                                    case "row":

                                    default:

                                }

                            }

                        });

                    }

                }

            }

        });

        return order;

    }

function execute() {



    var firstLevelDescription, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition,

        columnOrder, rowOrder, firstLevelCollection, linksCollection, columnCollection;



    var windowW = window.screen.width < 1024;

    var topLevelMenu = document.querySelector('[class*="hamburgerBtn"]') ? document.querySelectorAll('[class*="hamburgerBtn"]') : document.querySelectorAll('.fb-masthead__new-hamburger-menu [class*="_firstCategories"],[class*="CategoryMenuButton-module_menu-toggle-button"]');

    //var validateServer = digitalData.page.serverName;

    if (topLevelMenu.length === 0)

        return;

    document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {

        try {

                firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition() + 1;

                firstLevelDescription = ui.firstLevelDescription();

                var theParent = function() {

                    if (windowW) {

                        return linkTo;

                    } else {

                            return ui.isSLP() ? menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement : menuLink.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement

                        } else {

                            return menuLink.parentElement.parentElement;

                        }

                    }

                };

                secondLevelDescription = ui.secondLevelDescription(theParent());

                thirdLevelDescription = menuLink.textContent.trim() !== "" && menuLink.textContent.trim() !== "arrow" ? menuLink.textContent.trim() : secondLevelDescription;

                }

            }

            if (/img_banner/.test(event.target.className)) {

                firstLevelPosition = ui.firstLevelPosition();

                var topCategory = event.target.parentElement.parentElement.parentElement.closest('[class*="submenuStage"]').querySelector('[class*="FirstLevelItems_menuElementsHover"]').textContent;

                    localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                }

                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', topCategory + '|' + 'B1' + '|' + ImgName + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + '50' + '|' + '1');

            }

            if (event.target.closest('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_category-content-container"],[class*="CategoryMenuMobile-module_mobile-menu-container"]')) {

                if (window.screen.width < 1024) {

                    //dosomething

                        linksCollection = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category"]') ?                             return;

                        }

                        }

                    }

                } else {

                    if (event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') || ('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]')) {

                        columnCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[class*="SubCategories-module_tab-container"] ul'));

                        linksCollection = [].slice.apply(event.target.closest('ul').querySelectorAll('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]'));

                        firstLevelCollection = [].slice.apply(document.querySelectorAll('[data-testid="desktop-menu-category-button"]'))



                        firstLevelPosition = firstLevelCollection.indexOf(document.querySelector('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_active"]')) + 1;

                        firstLevelDescription = document.querySelector('[class*="CategoryMenuDesktop-module_active"] span').innerText;

                        columnOrder = columnCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('ul'));

                        secondLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText : event.target.closest('ul').querySelector('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText;

                        thirdLevelDescription = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]').innerText : event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]').innerText;

                        rowOrder = event.target.closest('[data-testid="second-level-category-link"]') ? 0 : linksCollection.indexOf(event.target.closest('[data-testid="third-level-category-link"]')) + 1;

                        if (_satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'home' || _satellite.getVar('page_pageName') === 'falabella home') {

                            localStorage.setItem('hometag', ui.str());

                            //sessionStorage.setItem('cyberString', ui.str(firstLevelDescription, firstLevelPosition, secondLevelDescription, thirdLevelDescription, columnOrder, rowOrder));



                        }

                        localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', firstLevelDescription + '|' + secondLevelDescription + '|' + thirdLevelDescription + '|' + firstLevelPosition + '|' + columnOrder + '|' + rowOrder);



                    }



                }

            }

            if (menuLink && windowW && !ui.approvedTrackClick(menuLink) && (menuLink.closest('li[class*="MenuUtils"]') || menuLink.querySelector('li[class*="MenuUtils"]'))) {



                var listElement = menuLink.closest('li[class*="MenuUtils"]') || menuLink.querySelector('li[class*="MenuUtils"]');

                var menuItems = Array.from(listElement.closest('ul').querySelectorAll('li[class*="MenuUtils"]'));

                var menuDescription = listElement.innerText.trim().replace(/\r?\n|\r/g, ' ');

                menuDescription = menuDescription.startsWith('Tienes') ? 'Mis CMR puntos' : menuDescription;



                localStorage.setItem('topLevelMenuCoords', menuDescription + '|' + menuDescription + '|' + menuDescription + '|' + 'H' + (menuItems.indexOf(listElement) + 1) + '|0|0');

            }



            if (_satellite && localStorage.getItem('topLevelMenuCoords') && isOutOfDomain(anchorLink)) {

                _satellite.track('OOD_CALL');

            }

        } catch (ex) {}

    });

}



execute();

  <script>_satellite["_runScript23"](function(event, target, Promise) {

//setInterval(checkSkuBasket, 100);



function checkSkuBasket() {

    var counter = 0;

    document.querySelectorAll('.fb-basket__order-container__details > .fb-product-item').forEach(function(el) {

        counter = counter + 1;

    });



    if (counter > 0) {

        hideBuyButton(counter);

    }

}



function hideBuyButton(int) {

    var buyButton = document.querySelectorAll('.fb-order-status__continue-purchase');

    if (int > 10) {

        buyButton.forEach(function(el) {

            el.classList.add('fb-btn-disabled');

            el.classList.remove('fb-btn-primary');



            el.style.pointerEvents = "none";

            el.parentNode.style.cursor = "not-allowed";

            createTextOrderStatus();

        })

    } else {

        buyButton.forEach(function(el) {

            el.classList.remove('fb-btn-disabled');

            el.classList.add('fb-btn-primary');

            el.style.pointerEvents = "auto";

            el.parentNode.style.cursor = "pointer";

            deleteTextOrderStatus();

        })



    }

}



function createTextOrderStatus() {

    var orderStatusArray = document.querySelector('.fb-order-status');

    if (!orderStatusArray.querySelector('.disableText')) {

        var disableTextContainer=document.createElement('div');

        disableTextContainer.classList.add('cyberday-warning-basket-container');

        var disableText = document.createElement('div');

        disableText.classList.add('fb-order-status__sub-totals__copy');

        disableText.classList.add('disableText');

      //<i class="alert-icon-warning-ux"></i>

        disableText.innerHTML = '<i class="alert-icon-warning-ux"></i> Para asegurar la mejor experiencia coloca como m\u00E1ximo 10 productos en tu bolsa.\nSi tienes m\u00E1s productos col\u00F3calos en una nueva orden.';

        disableTextContainer.appendChild(disableText)

        orderStatusArray.appendChild(disableTextContainer);

    }



}



function deleteTextOrderStatus() {

    var orderStatusArray = document.querySelectorAll('.fb-order-status');

    orderStatusArray.forEach(function(el) {

        if (el.querySelector('.cyberday-warning-basket-container')) {

            el.querySelector('.cyberday-warning-basket-container').remove();

        }

    });

  

  



}

});</script>
